shared_focus = {
	id = FEA_economy
	icon = GFX_goal_feathisia_money
	cost = 1.50
	ai_will_do = { factor = 500 }
	x = 5
	y = 0
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus FEA_economy"
		add_political_power = 30
		country_event = { 
		    id = feat.1 
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = FEA_government_intervention
	icon = GFX_goal_tfv_saf_anti_colonialist_crusade
	x = -2
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = FEA_economy
	cost = 4.40
	available = { has_country_flag = FEA_government_intervention_flag }
	prerequisite = { focus = FEA_economy }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = FEA_free_market }

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 500
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus FEA_government_intervention"
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = FEA_crashed_economy
			add_idea = FEA_gov_inter
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { days = 50 id = feat.19 }
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

	icon = GFX_goal_constitutional_guarantees
	x = 0
	y = 4
	relative_position_id = FEA_government_intervention
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = FEA_buyout_noble_assets }
	prerequisite = { focus = FEA_nationalize_industries }

		}

		}

								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory

		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = FEA_industrial_planning
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_soviet_construction
	x = 3
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = FEA_red_dawn

			is_controlled_by = ROOT

				include_locked = yes
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 120
	}

			limit = {

					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes

shared_focus = {
	id = FEA_industrial_democracy
	icon = GFX_goal_munitions_factories
	x = -8
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = FEA_party_convention
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = FEA_kogchel_socialists }
	available = {
		has_government = communism
		any_owned_state = {
			is_controlled_by = ROOT
			free_building_slots = {
				building = industrial_complex
				size > 0
				include_locked = yes
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 120
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus FEA_industrial_democracy"
		add_ideas = FEA_workplace_democracy
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = FEA_PYT_dealing
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_dangerous_deal
	x = -3
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = FEA_the_throne
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = FEA_protection_alliance }
	bypass = {
		OR = {
			has_war_with = PYT
			PYT = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
	}

	will_lead_to_war_with = PYT

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus FEA_PYT_dealing"
		if = {
			limit = { PYT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			PYT = { country_event = { id = imperial.32 days = 10 } }
			else = { create_wargoal = { target = PYT type = annex_everything } }
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = FEA_BRZ_and_STW
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_major_alliance
	x = -1
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = FEA_the_throne
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = FEA_protection_alliance }

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	bypass = {
		AND = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = BRZ
				BRZ = {
					exists = no
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_war_with = STW
				STW = {
					exists = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	will_lead_to_war_with = STW
	will_lead_to_war_with = BRZ

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus FEA_BRZ_and_STW"
		if = {
			limit = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			STW = { country_event = { id = imperial.31 days = 10 } }
			else = { create_wargoal = { target = STW type = annex_everything } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { BRZ = { exists = yes is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			BRZ = { country_event = { id = imperial.32 days = 10 } }
			else = { create_wargoal = { target = BRZ type = annex_everything } }
		}
	}
}
